## Analysis

The Ground Truth (GT) is:
$$-0.2597\sqrt{A} + 0.9123\cos(\log(A + 1))$$

Let me check the candidates systematically.

**Candidate 19:** `sqrt(A)*c0 + c1 + c2*cos(c3*log(A*c4 + 1))`

Setting:
- c0 = -0.2597 (coefficient of √A)
- c1 = 0 (no constant offset in GT)
- c2 = 0.9123 (coefficient of cos term)
- c3 = 1 (coefficient inside log)
- c4 = 1 (coefficient of A inside log, giving log(A + 1))

This gives: $-0.2597\sqrt{A} + 0 + 0.9123\cos(1 \cdot \log(A \cdot 1 + 1)) = -0.2597\sqrt{A} + 0.9123\cos(\log(A+1))$

This matches the GT exactly! ✓

**Candidate 16:** `sqrt(A)*c0 + c1 + c2*sin(c3*log(A*c4 + 1) + c5)`

Setting:
- c0 = -0.2597
- c1 = 0
- c2 = 0.9123
- c3 = 1
- c4 = 1
- c5 = π/2 (since sin(x + π/2) = cos(x))

This also gives: $-0.2597\sqrt{A} + 0.9123\sin(\log(A+1) + \pi/2) = -0.2597\sqrt{A} + 0.9123\cos(\log(A+1))$

This also matches! ✓

**Candidate 15:** `A**c0*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6)`

Setting c0 = 0.5 gives A^0.5 = √A, so:
- c0 = 0.5, c1 = -0.2597, c2 = 0, c3 = 0.9123, c4 = 1, c5 = 1, c6 = π/2

This matches as well. ✓

**Candidate 17:** `A**c0*c1 + c2 + c3*cos(c4*log(A**c5*c6 + 1))`

Setting c0 = 0.5, c1 = -0.2597, c2 = 0, c3 = 0.9123, c4 = 1, c5 = 1, c6 = 1:

This gives: $-0.2597\sqrt{A} + 0.9123\cos(\log(A+1))$ ✓

Multiple candidates match, with **Candidate 19** being the most direct and clean match.
